 The pattern of GST that is emerging after three council meetings is not to raise expectations, but to raise fears:  The central government has proposed four rates for Goods and Services Tax in the GST Council meeting
 ye daren 6, 12,18 or 26 fisadi hongi
 The rate for gold will be four per cent separately

  In the current system, many goods and products of common consumption are exempt from VAT or excise duty
 kuch utpaadon par 3, 5 or 9 fisadi waite lagata he jabaki kuch par 6 fisadi exise duty he
 Under the GST tax system, all products with 3 to 9 per cent VAT and 6 per cent excise will be under the first GST rate of 6 per cent
 jiro duty saamaan kii pranali shaayad nahin rahegi isliye tex kii yah dar mahangaai badhaane kii taraf jhuki ho sakati he

 yah anokhaa or apratyaashit he

 yah jiesti main pechidagi kaa nayaa charam he
 ह There is no harm in assuming that most of the products and services will be under the 18 per cent rate because GST has a uniform rate system for goods and services as per the international system
 is vyavastha ke tahat sevaaon par tex dar vartmaan ke 15 fisadi (ses sahit) se badhkar 18 fisadi ho jaaegi

 haal hi main hue raashtrapati chunaav main gayum ke sautele bhai abdullayaminahaar gaye the
 Gayoom (80) and his son elected representative Ferris Maumoon were released on bail by the High Court in Male
 abdulla yamin kii ek saptaah pehle hue chunaavon main karaari shikast hui thi
 Gayoom's daughter and former foreign minister, Dunya, welcomed the release, saying that he hoped that the punishment of other political prisoners, including former President Mohammad Nasheed, would also be withdrawn
 gayum ke ghar lautne ke baad moumun ne maale se phone par bataaya, 'ye sabhi raajnneetik rup se prerit dosha-siddhiyaan hai or mujhe aashaa he ki unhen bhi jald waapas liya jayega, jisase nashid bhi ghar lautenge
 Nasheed, the first democratically elected president in the country, was sentenced to 13 years of imprisonment in 2015 on terrorism charges
 unhen 2016 main jail se chuttee lee thi or vah ilaaj ke liye landan gayi the or tab se videsh main hi hai
 Ibrahim Mohammad Solih was supported by both Nasheed and Gayoom to challenge Yameen
 navnirvaachit raashtrapati solih ne yamin se sabhi raajnneetik kaidiyon ko reeha karne kii apil kii thi
 Gayoom ruled the Maldives for 30 consecutive years in the 340,000 Sunni Muslims
 vah 2008 main desh ke pehle bahudaleey chunaav main haarane ke baad satta se hate the
 He had helped his half-brother Yameen win in the 2013 election, but the two brothers subsequently had a big rift
 gayum ko desh ke pradhan nyaayadhish or ucchtam nyaayalay ke ek anya nyaayadhish ke saath yamin kii sarkaar ko giraane ke prayaas ke aarope main is saal farvari main giraftaar kar liya gaya tha
 These big leaders of the country were serving a sentence of 19 months imprisonment for obstructing justice
